The function iterates through URL segments (host, port, path, query, anchor) in reverse order using `_URL_SEGMENTS` (lines 559-580).\n\n4. Key issue: Lines 562-579 use `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` which decodes percent-encoded characters. This is the root cause of the first bug.\n\nFor example, when getting the path, it uses:\n```python\nlambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n```\n\nThis will decode `%3A` (encoded colon) to `:` and `%20` (encoded space) to a space. Then the regex is applied to the decoded string. So when incrementing `http://localhost/%3A5`, it decodes to `http://localhost/:5`, and the regex finds the `5` and increments it, potentially also modifying the `:` part if the regex captures it incorrectly.\n\nLet me check the test file to understand what the expected behavior should %35 decodes to '5', so %355 becomes '55' internally\n        # When incremented, it should become '56'\n        # The result should preserve the encoding correctly\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n        # The result should still have the %35 preserved and only the last digit changed\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # This will fail because the code improperly decodes %35 to 5\n        # %3A should remain as %3A (representing ':')\n        # Only the trailing 5 should become 6\n        assert result_str == \"http://localhost/%3A6\", (\n            f\"Expected http://localhost/%3A6, got {result_str}\"\n        )\n        assert '%3A' in result_str, (\n            f\"BUG: %3A encoding was corrupted in: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n\nclass TestNegativeValueHandling:\n    \"\"\"Test that negative values are properly rejected.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing 1 by 2 raises an error.\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/page_1\")\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError) as excinfo:\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=2, segments={'path'})\n        assert \"Can't decrement\" in excinfo.value.msg\n\n    def test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing doesn't produce negative numbers.\n\n        This test verifies the bug: decrementing URL with small number\n        should raise an error, not allow negative values.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/image_2\")\n        # The regex pattern is then applied to the decoded string, losing information about which digits were originally encoded.\n\n---\n\n### Bug 2: URL-Encoded Data Is Lost/Corrupted\n**Tests**: \n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_space_in_path`\n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_multiple_encoded_sequences`  \n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_unicode_character`\n- `TestComplexScenarios::test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space`\n\n**Issue**: URL-encoded characters (spaces, Unicode, special characters) are decoded but when the path is set back using `StrictMode`, it rejects literal spaces and other characters, resulting in invalid URLs.\n\n**Examples**:\n1. Input: `http://example.com/my%20file/5` (space encoded as %20)\n   - Decoded internally to: `http://example.com/my file/5`\n   - After operation: URL becomes invalid (empty string)\n   - Expected: `http://example.com/my%20file/6` (encoding preserved)\n\n2. Input: `http://example.com/%C3%A4/5` (encoded Unicode 'ä')\n   - Result: `http://example.com/ä/6` (literal character instead of encoding)\n   - Expected: `http://example.com/%C3%A4/6` (encoding preserved)\n\n**Root Cause**: The getters use `QUrl.PrettyDecoded`, which decodes certain characters. When the modified string is set back with `QUrl.StrictMode`, it:\n- Rejects literal spaces (invalid in URLs)\n- Converts Unicode characters to their literal form instead of re-encoding\n- Creates invalid or corrupted URLs\n\n---\n\n### Bug 3: Negative Values After Decrement\n**Tests**:\n- `TestNegativeValueHandling::test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit`\n- `TestNegativeValueHandling::test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative`\n\n**Status**: ✅ PASSING - This bug is NOT present in the current code\n\n**Verification**: The code correctly raises `IncDecError` when attempting to decrement below 0:\n```python\nif val < count:\n    raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count), url)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Test Results on Buggy Code\n\n```\n===== Test Results =====\nPASSED:  5 tests\n- test_encoded_colon_with_trailing_number\n- test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit\n- test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative\n- test_encoded_percent_character\n- test_increment_in_query_with_encoded_equals\n\nFAILED:  5 tests\n- test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number\n  Error: BUG: Encoded sequence %35 was corrupted!\n  \n- test_encoded_space_in_path\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n  \n- test_multiple_encoded_sequences\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n  \n- test_encoded_unicode_character\n  Error: BUG: Encoded Unicode %C3%A4 was corrupted!\n  \n- test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n```\n\n---\n\n## Technical Details\n\n### Problematic Code Section\n**File**: `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py` (lines 559-626)\n\nThe `_URL_SEGMENTS` tuple (lines 559-580) uses `PrettyDecoded` mode:\n```python\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    ('path', lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),\n    ('query', lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),\n    ...\n]\n```\n\nThis decodes percent-encoded sequences, and the regex pattern:\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)', getter(url))\n```\n\nCannot properly distinguish between:\n- Digits that were originally encoded (e.g., from `%35`)\n- Digits that are actual number values to increment\n\n### Why This Is Problematic\n\n1. **Loss of Information**: `PrettyDecoded` removes encoding context needed by the regex\n2. **Invalid URL Creation**: `StrictMode` setters reject literal spaces and other characters that were decoded\n3. **Regex Ineffectiveness**: The negative lookahead `(?<!%)(?<!%.)` cannot prevent matching digits in encoded sequences because they're already decoded\n\n---\n\n## How to Fix (Design Notes)\n\nThe fix would need to:\n1. **Preserve Encoding**: Use `QUrl.FullyEncoded` or a mode that preserves percent-encoding\n2. **Avoid Decoding**: Apply regex to encoded form, then map matches back to original positions\n3. **Safe Re-encoding**: Use appropriate encoding when setting values back\n4. **Proper Mode Selection**: Use appropriate QUrl encoding mode when setting segments\n\n---\n\n## Files\n- **Test File**: `/workspace/regression_test.py`\n- **Implementation**: `/app/qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py`\n- **Test Framework**: pytest with PyQt5\n\n---\n\n## Execution\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py -v\n```\n\nThe tests are self-contained and do not require additional configuration files.\nEOF\ncat The regex pattern is then applied to the decoded string, losing information about which digits were originally encoded.\n\n---\n\n### Bug 2: URL-Encoded Data Is Lost/Corrupted\n**Tests**: \n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_space_in_path`\n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_multiple_encoded_sequences`  \n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_unicode_character`\n- `TestComplexScenarios::test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space`\n\n**Issue**: URL-encoded characters (spaces, Unicode, special characters) are decoded but when the path is set back using `StrictMode`, it rejects literal spaces and other characters, resulting in invalid URLs.\n\n**Examples**:\n1. Input: `http://example.com/my%20file/5` (space encoded as %20)\n   - Decoded internally to: `http://example.com/my file/5`\n   - After operation: URL becomes invalid (empty string)\n   - Expected: `http://example.com/my%20file/6` (encoding preserved)\n\n2. Input: `http://example.com/%C3%A4/5` (encoded Unicode 'ä')\n   - Result: `http://example.com/ä/6` (literal character instead of encoding)\n   - Expected: `http://example.com/%C3%A4/6` (encoding preserved)\n\n**Root Cause**: The getters use `QUrl.PrettyDecoded`, which decodes certain characters. When the modified string is set back with `QUrl.StrictMode`, it:\n- Rejects literal spaces (invalid in URLs)\n- Converts Unicode characters to their literal form instead of re-encoding\n- Creates invalid or corrupted URLs\n\n---\n\n### Bug 3: Negative Values After Decrement\n**Tests**:\n- `TestNegativeValueHandling::test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit`\n- `TestNegativeValueHandling::test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative`\n\n**Status**: ✅ PASSING - This bug is NOT present in the current code\n\n**Verification**: The code correctly raises `IncDecError` when attempting to decrement below 0:\n```python\nif val < count:\n    raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count), url)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Test Results on Buggy Code\n\n```\n===== Test Results =====\nPASSED:  5 tests\n- test_encoded_colon_with_trailing_number\n- test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit\n- test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative\n- test_encoded_percent_character\n- test_increment_in_query_with_encoded_equals\n\nFAILED:  5 tests\n- test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number\n  Error: BUG: Encoded sequence %35 was corrupted!\n  \n- test_encoded_space_in_path\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n  \n- test_multiple_encoded_sequences\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n  \n- test_encoded_unicode_character\n  Error: BUG: Encoded Unicode %C3%A4 was corrupted!\n  \n- test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n```\n\n---\n\n## Technical Details\n\n### Problematic Code Section\n**File**: `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py` (lines 559-626)\n\nThe `_URL_SEGMENTS` tuple (lines 559-580) uses `PrettyDecoded` mode:\n```python\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    ('path', lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),\n    ('query', lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),\n    ...\n]\n```\n\nThis decodes percent-encoded sequences, and the regex pattern:\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)', getter(url))\n```\n\nCannot properly distinguish between:\n- Digits that were originally encoded (e.g., from `%35`)\n- Digits that are actual number values to increment\n\n### Why This Is Problematic\n\n1. **Loss of Information**: `PrettyDecoded` removes encoding context needed by the regex\n2. **Invalid URL Creation**: `StrictMode` setters reject literal spaces and other characters that were decoded\n3. **Regex Ineffectiveness**: The negative lookahead `(?<!%)(?<!%.)` cannot prevent matching digits in encoded sequences because they're already decoded\n\n---\n\n## How to Fix (Design Notes)\n\nThe fix would need to:\n1. **Preserve Encoding**: Use `QUrl.FullyEncoded` or a mode that preserves percent-encoding\n2. **Avoid Decoding**: Apply regex to encoded form, then map matches back to original positions\n3. **Safe Re-encoding**: Use appropriate encoding when setting values back\n4. **Proper Mode Selection**: Use appropriate QUrl encoding mode when setting segments\n\n---\n\n## Files\n- **Test File**: `/workspace/regression_test.py`\n- **Implementation**: `/app/qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py`\n- **Test Framework**: pytest with PyQt5\n\n---\n\n## Execution\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py -v\n```\n\nThe tests are self-contained and do not require additional configuration
